  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',

        state: 'apple_oauth_state_3338948b-f584-420e-83f1-e9cdd64b5632'

<div id="descriptionContainer">
  
      <div id="description" class="readable stacked" style="right:0">
        
<span id="freeTextContainer9757398585737292502"><b>Dive into a world torn apart by a powerful race with phenomenal powers of the mind— and none of the heart…</b><br/><br/>In a world that denies emotions, where the ruling Psy punish any sign of desire, Sascha Duncan must conceal the feelings that brand her as flawed. To reveal them would be to sentence herself to the horror of “rehabilitation”— the complete psychic erasure of everything </span>
  <span id="freeText9757398585737292502" style="display:none"><b>Dive into a world torn apart by a powerful race with phenomenal powers of the mind— and none of the heart…</b><br /><br />In a world that denies emotions, where the ruling Psy punish any sign of desire, Sascha Duncan must conceal the feelings that brand her as flawed. To reveal them would be to sentence herself to the horror of “rehabilitation”— the complete psychic erasure of everything she ever was….<br /><br />Both human and animal, Lucas Hunter is a Changeling hungry for the very sensations the Psy disdain. After centuries of uneasy co-existence, these two races are now on the verge of war over the brutal murders of several Changeling women. Lucas is determined to find the Psy killer who butchered his packmate, and Sascha is his ticket into their closely guarded society. But he soon discovers that this ice-cold Psy is very capable of passion—and that the animal in him is fascinated by her. Caught between their conflicting worlds, Lucas and Sascha must remain bound to their identities—or sacrifice everything for a taste of darkest temptation…</span>
  <a data-text-id="9757398585737292502" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      </div>
</div>

<div class='communityQuestionAndAnswer'>
<div class='communityQuestion'>
<div class='questionText'>
<a href="/questions/735603-so-i-ve-read-the-entire-series-numerous">So...I&#39;ve read the entire series, numerous times. Now I&#39;m looking for something as addictive. The same realm of PNR, even the same formula of couple per book. Any recommendations? As long as it&#39;s good writing and engaging characters, I&#39;m all game to try it.</a>
</div>
<div class='communityQAFooter questionFooter'>
<ul class='questionFooterActions'>
<li class='footerItem like'>
<span class='likeItContainer' id='like_container_community_question_735603'><a id="like_count_community_question_735603" rel="nofollow" href="/rating/voters/735603?resource_type=CommunityQuestion"><span class="likesCount">32 likes</span></a>&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;<a rel="nofollow" class="jsLike like_it" href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/new?remember=true&amp;return_url=%2Fbook%2Fshow%2F178476.Slave_to_Sensation">like</a></span>

</li>
<li class='footerItem communityQuestionTimestamp'>
<a href="/questions/735603-so-i-ve-read-the-entire-series-numerous">4 years ago</a>
</li>
<li class='footerItem communityQuestionPermalink'>
<a href="/questions/735603-so-i-ve-read-the-entire-series-numerous">See all 7 answers</a>
</li>
</ul>
</div>

</div>
<div class='allCommunityAnswers'>
<div class='communityAnswer'>
<div class='communityAnswerBody'>
<div class='answererUserIcon'>
<a class="leftAlignedImage userPhoto" href="/user/show/33970958-brit"><img alt="" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/users/1518845592i/33970958._UX100_CR0,29,100,100_.jpg" /></a>
</div>
<div class='communityAnswerTextContainer'>
<span class='communityAnswererName'>
<a href="/user/show/33970958-brit">Brit</a>
</span>
<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">Ok so this is a huge list - but I promise all the books listed really great or at least very good if not great)<br/><br/>Elder Races - Thea Harrison (The MOST s<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">Ok so this is a huge list - but I promise all the books listed really great or at least very good if not great)<br /><br />Elder Races - Thea Harrison (The MOST similar to psy-changeling series in my opinion...)<br />Immortals After Dark by Kresley Cole is a close second...although some of the books beat psy-changeling books in my opinion (same with Elder Races)...also the novellas for Thea Harrison are seriously amazing, just like psy-changeling novellas are great. (Also, this series is great in audio)<br /><br />Kingmaker - Amanda Bouchet<br /><br />K.f. Breene - ALL her books but in order from favorite to (still great but..)less favorite - Fire and Ice, Darkness, Fate of Perfection, Warrior Chronicles... but really all these are FUN reads! And the first 3 series listed are not only cool PNR but funny too!<br /><br />Burn in You- suzanne Collins (more interesting and likeable characters than Phoenix pack series by the same author...plus great romance and really funny)<br /><br />Kate Daniels - Ilona Andrews<br /><br />Poison Study(and spin off series) - Maria V. Snyder - LOVE LOVE! (Also this is a great series to listen to on audio)<br /><br />Graceling series - Kristen Cashore - highly recommend! <br /><br />Court of Thorns and Roses - Sarah J Maas (AMAZING book 2 and 3, and better than Throne of Glass series, which I highly recommend also)<br /><br />Walker Saga - Jaymin Eve (really interesting world, and like this series each book has new main characters)<br /><br />Charley Davidson - Darynda Jones (Awesome series with so many LOL moments)<br /><br />Seven Realms - Cinda Williams Chima (OMG you will love this series!)<br />OMG how could I forget - Immortals after Dark is AWESOME AWESOME AWESOME! Definitely start with "A war lord wants forever, I think its listed as .5) (Also, this series is great in audio)<br /><br />Fae Chronicles - Amelia Hutchins ( really really recommend this series, LOL moments, fun world, no annoying characters...just really great.<br /><br />Ollie Witt - Donna Augustine (only 1 book out but a good start to a series that I am sure will be great)<br /><br />Pride - Shelley Laurensten (the world and characters are more fun than serious and definitely LOL moments here and there)<br /><br />Bargainer - Laura Thalassa (1 book out so far but the second book to be released soon) - This is also a top pick..<br /><br />Dragons of Bloodfire - Erin Kellison (I loved book 1 and enjoyed book 2, I am not sure why it isn't more popular but, in my opinion I really liked it, and if you have read through the suggestions thus far and agree with me about the ones you have read, then I say...trust me and not the mixed review for this series)<br /><br />The Remnant Chronicles - Mary Pearson (This series was amazeballs! AND the series is complete so you can read it straight through without waiting for the next in the series to be released.)<br /><br />An Ember in the Ashes - Sabaa Tahir (GREAT start to a series)<br /><br />Vampire Academy - another series that is complete.<br /><br />Starbound and Illuminae Files - Amie Kaufman (more sci-fi than paranormal but definitely good reads)Nightwalker - Jacquelyn Frank (I loved this series, but World of Nightwalker series is really bad! and her stand alones aren't great either. but THIS series I highly recommend. AND the series is complete - so no waiting)<br /><br />Both C.L Wilson series - Tairen Soul series is complete. Weathermages series book 1 was really good, but the second book is seriously taking forever, which is really annoying...<br />And just some other series to check into - <br /><br />Seven - Dannika Dark<br /><br />Immortal Guardians and The Gifted Ones - Dianne Duvall<br /><br />Black Daggar Brotherhood - alot of people LOVE this series but I think its good, not great)<br /><br />Lords of Underworld - Gena Showalter<br /><br />Kricket - Amy Bartel (series complete)<br /><br />The Black Mage - Rachel E. Carter (series complete and book 1 is so much less than the rest of the series, so if you start this series and are unsure if you want to continue, DO continue because the rest of the series gets better with every book).<br /><br />Blood Destiny - Helen Harper<br /><br />Fever - Karen Marie Moning<br /><br />Merry Gentry - Laurell K Hamilton - VERY graphic sex and erotica (just warning you)<br /><br />A few standalones - <br />Firebird - Susanna Kearsley(the audiobook is AMAZING - irish accents!!)<br />Anything by Marissa Meyer!!<br />The Duke of Shadows - Meredith Duran - some really memorable moments and a sweet romance<br /><br />Ok these are NOT PNR but still HIGHLY RECOMMENDED -<br /><br />Maiden Lane - Elizabeth Hoyt (books 3 on are my favorites, you dont necessarily need to read in order)<br /><br />Neighbors from Hell - Hilarious series and the book that is the 1 historical romance (the original family) is so so funny with the sweetest romance and ending!<br /><br />I hope I have given you many choices that you have not already read! Please let me know your opinion on my suggestions!<a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>
</div>

<div class='communityQuestion'>
<div class='questionText'>
<a href="/questions/388927-do-you-have-to-read-the-entire-series-in">Do you have to read the entire series in order, or are they good stand alones? I&#39;m kind of hesitant to start such a long series!</a>
</div>
<div class='communityQAFooter questionFooter'>

<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">In my opinion, the first few books could act as stand-alones though you won't get the full effect, however, the story line gets more complex as it goe<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">In my opinion, the first few books could act as stand-alones though you won't get the full effect, however, the story line gets more complex as it goes on so you probably should read them all in order. I absolutely love this series and would definitely recommend it! <a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>

    <a title="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake"><img alt="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1605987751p2/11626803.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/385609855?book_show_action=true">Aug 06, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" href="/user/show/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake">Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake?shelf=can-shit-on-paper-i-would-read-it">can-shit-on-paper-i-would-read-it</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer385609855" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10172472660436527494"><b><i>***Updated for book 19***</i><br/><br/>This is the kick starter for one of my <b>FAVORITE</b> UF/PNR series of all time.</b> <br/><br/>ALL.<br/><br/>FUCKING.<br/><br/>TIME, people. <br/><br/>If you love paranormal romance and/or urban fantasy, look no further than this series. <br/><br/>Look no further than Nalini Singh.<br/><br/>Her writing is flawless. <br/>Her world building is incredible.<br/>And her characters and story lines are in a league of their own. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1494084579ra/22683726.gif' width='500' height='209' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>LOLZ.<br/><br/>See what I did there?<br/><br/>Side note: I actually have a love/hate relationship with this movie. When you played softball for 16+ ye</span>
  <span id="freeText10172472660436527494" style="display:none"><b><i>***Updated for book 19***</i><br><br>This is the kick starter for one of my <b>FAVORITE</b> UF/PNR series of all time.</b> <br><br>ALL.<br><br>FUCKING.<br><br>TIME, people. <br><br>If you love paranormal romance and/or urban fantasy, look no further than this series. <br><br>Look no further than Nalini Singh.<br><br>Her writing is flawless. <br>Her world building is incredible.<br>And her characters and story lines are in a league of their own. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1494084579ra/22683726.gif" width="500" height="209" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>LOLZ.<br><br>See what I did there?<br><br>Side note: I actually have a love/hate relationship with this movie. When you played softball for 16+ years like I did?<br><br>Believe me, you've SEEN <i>A League of Their Own</i> way more than any one person ever should in their lifetime. <br><br>Almost to its detriment. <br><br>But anybadjoke, back to this book and Nalini Singh's awesomeness. <br><br>This book is the beginning of a true PNR saga of legit proportions. <br><br>In this book, you are introduced to some changelings (shifters) and what I think is a truly brilliant and utterly original people (at least <i>I</i> had never read about anything like it before): <br><br>The Psy race and the thing they call "Silence."<br><br>Will it blow your PNR mind?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1494084579i/22683727.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Not only that, but in this book, we are introduced to one of my favorite book husbands of all time:<br>Lucas Hunter. <br><br>Seriously though, I love this series so much, I am LEGIT pimping it out right now. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1494084579ra/22683728.gif" width="480" height="360" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I just can't say enough good things about it. <br><br>And ya'll know I'm not one to gush too much. <br><br>If you haven't read it, you fucking should. <br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1494084579i/22683729.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>On a series setup side note:<br><br>After reading this one, some people get concerned that EVERY book will be a Male Changeling / Female Psy coupling - because both Book One and Book Two both are - and since I've been asked numerous times by various friends who are just starting out in this series if such is the case, I decided to list a breakdown of the coupling types for the series up to its current point (<i>Silver Silence</i>). <br><br>So, for those interested:<br><br>Book 1 (Psy-Changeling) - Male Changeling (DarkRiver Alpha)/Female Psy<br>Book 2 - Male Changeling (DarkRiver)/Female Psy (<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/386120641" rel="nofollow noopener">Visions of Heat</a>)<br>Book 3 - Male SnowDancer Psy/Female Changeling (SnowDancer) (<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/385600129" rel="nofollow noopener">Caressed by Ice</a>)<br>Book 4 - Male Changeling (DarkRiver)/Human Female (<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/386120728" rel="nofollow noopener">Mine to Possess</a>)<br>Book 5 - Male Changeling (DarkRiver)/Female Psy (Hostage to Pleasure)<br>Book 6 - Male Changeling (SnowDancer)/Female Changeling (DarkRiver) (Branded by Fire)<br>Book 7 - Male Human / Female Psy (Blaze of Memory)<br>Book 8 - Male Human Cop/Female Justice Psy (Bonds of Justice)<br>Book 9 - Male AND Female SnowDancer Changelings (Play of Passion)<br>Book 10 - Male Changeling (SnowDancer Alpha)/Female SnowDancer Psy (<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/908273384" rel="nofollow noopener">Kiss of Snow</a>)<br>Book 11 - Male Changeling (SnowDancer) / Female Changeling (<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/390404993" rel="nofollow noopener">Tangle of Need</a>)<br>Book 12 - Male AND Female Psy (<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/496012820" rel="nofollow noopener">Heart of Obsidian</a>)<br>Book 13 - Male AND Female Psy (<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/923659014" rel="nofollow noopener">Shield of Winter</a>)<br>Book 14 - Male AND Female Psy (<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/923659540" rel="nofollow noopener">Shards of Hope</a>)<br><br>Book 15 (<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1449576072" rel="nofollow noopener">Alleigiance of Honor</a>)- NO focal couple. This books acts as a bridge between season one of the story arc (books 1 - 14) and season two (books 15+). While this book doesn't focus on any particular couple, it's a must-read for the series. <br><br>Book 16 (PC) (Trinity Book 1) - Male Changeling (StoneWater Alpha)/Female Psy (<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1947485233" rel="nofollow noopener">Silver Silence</a>)<br>Book 17 (PC) (Trinity Book 2) - Male Human/Female Changeling (BlackSea) (<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2114346549" rel="nofollow noopener">Ocean Light</a>)<br>Book 18 (PC) (Trinity Book 3) - Male Changeling (SnowDancer)/Female Psy (<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2733201002" rel="nofollow noopener">Wolf Rain</a>)<br>Book 19 (PC) (Trinity Book 4) - Female Changeling (BlackEdge Alpha)/Male Psy (<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3252399615" rel="nofollow noopener">Alpha Night</a>)<br><br>I don't know if this helps anyone out, but I thought I'd share. <br><br>Plus, I just like making lists...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423763635i/13669005._SY540_.jpg" width="540" height="577" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Anyway, like I said, if you haven't read this, go. <br><br>GO already.</span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_166610336" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/166610336" />
    <a title="Kat Kennedy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3270188-kat-kennedy"><img alt="Kat Kennedy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1537750381p2/3270188.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/166610336?book_show_action=true">May 08, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kat Kennedy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kat Kennedy" href="/user/show/3270188-kat-kennedy">Kat Kennedy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3270188-kat-kennedy?shelf=romance-romance-romance">romance-romance-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3270188-kat-kennedy?shelf=kat-s-book-reviews">kat-s-book-reviews</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer166610336" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7043106697872262337">This is a romance novel. If you're unfamiliar with the romance formula then I'm about to spoil every single romance novel ever:<br/><br/>They all end on a deliriously happy note with an abundance of perfection.<br/><br/>So whilst I won't discuss the actual end to this book, I don't think I really will be spoiling everything if I discuss the TYPE of end this book has and why it means that I just wasn't really meant for the romance genre.<br/><br/>There was a lot to enjoy about this book. For starters, considering it is billed</span>
  <span id="freeText7043106697872262337" style="display:none">This is a romance novel. If you're unfamiliar with the romance formula then I'm about to spoil every single romance novel ever:<br><br>They all end on a deliriously happy note with an abundance of perfection.<br><br>So whilst I won't discuss the actual end to this book, I don't think I really will be spoiling everything if I discuss the TYPE of end this book has and why it means that I just wasn't really meant for the romance genre.<br><br>There was a lot to enjoy about this book. For starters, considering it is billed as a romance novel, its world building was rather impressive. The "Psys" (people with specialized psychic/mental abilities), "Changelings" (shifters of various animal varieties) and humans all live together with Psys generally occupying the higher echelons of society.<br><br>The Psys are supposed to be completely unemotional and rational.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379789937i/529439.jpg" alt="Spock" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>Which generally means they live long and prosper!</i><br><br>While Changelings are moving up the social ladder leaving the humans in the gutter... where presumably they belong. I'm not sure - they don't feature much in this novel and I must say, as a human, I find this pretty offensive. The sole token human in the novel barely has a part!<br><br>Okay - so emotions are forbidden which makes things kind of awkward for resident Psy, Sascha Duncan and Alpha Changeling hunk, Lucas Hunter.<br><br>Luckily, it's a romance novel so they naturally work through it.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380349555i/703513.jpg" alt="or else..." class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>Or else...</i><br><br>My issue is that I just obviously wasn't really meant for the romance genre because I was perfectly fine with this book up until the last couple of chapters. I don't want a super happy ending. Not if it doesn't make any bloody sense and just comes out of nowhere. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380349555i/703514.jpg" alt="happy endings" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Also, I have more issues with paranormal romance and that is because most of them have a "mate for life" policy in which the paranormal creatures actually CAN'T mate with anyone else - even if their spouse dies.<br><br>Look, this isn't even true in nature. First of all, not all wolves mate for life in the wild - usually only an alpha pair. And you know what - if one of that pair dies, the other one will probably find another mate!<br><br>It's kind of a sick thing to romantizice over too, when you think about it. "He loves me so much, that if I died, he'd rather abandon our children and the world to come join me."<br><br>I don't think that's romantic at all. In fact, I think it qualifies as a very unhealthy relationship!<br><br>There were definite dominance and control issues in this story that annoyed me as well. Because, you know, the man is always right and a woman can't choose to make a sacrifice for something she believes in. That's just not right. She should listen to her man. She needs permission to do these things.<br><br>What is it with that in today's literature? Do we still want a man that's going to knock us unconscious just to retain control? <br><br>Okay, story time with Kat:<br><br>I'm pregnant and am therefor clinically insane. Mr Kennedy arrived home from work a few weeks ago to find me in the backyard tilling the soil.<br><br>"What the hell are you doing?!" he exclaimed angrily.<br><br>I glanced up from my hard labour, puffing but excited. "Look, honey! I'm making a veggie patch! Now we'll have nice fresh veggies to eat!"<br><br>Mr Kennedy looked at me with a special kind of horror as he began to mentally tabulate exactly how many more weeks this madness was likely to go on for. <br><br>"You hate gardening! Why would you want a veggie patch? Why, Honey? Why??!!"<br><br>I laughed at his silliness. Everyone needs a veggie patch. Silly, silly man! "Oh! It'll be fun! I'll just finish tilling this soil and then we can go out right away and buy some seedlings! We'll have nice fresh veggies by the time the baby comes!"<br><br>Mr Kennedy now has a Pavlovian upchuck reflex to any sentence that ends in, "...by the time the baby comes!" There is a certain manic way pregnant women say that, which instantly informs the rest of the world that reason and logic no longer hold any value.<br><br>I then began furiously churning up the soil with one of those pick-axe-like things that you use to do this kind of work. I don't know really, I found it in the shed and it looked like it'd do the job. I think I've seen someone use it in a movie.<br><br>"Will you stop that! You're pregnant!"<br><br>"Don't be silly, I'll be done soon, darling!"<br><br>Mr Kennedy groaned before stripping off his work shirt, snatching the pick-axe from me and saying, "Fine, I'll do it! You just go sit down over there!"<br><br>It was at this point that I could KIND of understand why my female ancestors traded some of their freedom and rights if it meant getting to watch a man like him work in the field every day.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380349555i/703515.jpg" alt="the sexy" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>Because frankly, he looks a lot like this. And he was very, very impressive... with that pick-axe...</i><br><br>But I'm crazy, and pregnant and hormones are what they are.<br><br>The fact is though, that as crazy and pregnant and hormonal as I am, I still don't want a caveman who thinks he can threaten, control, dominate and bully me. Though I have consistently made sure I'm doing heavy work around the time Mr Kennedy gets home so that I can watch him do it instead, no man is hot enough to be ordering me around and stomping all over my free-will, damn it!<br><br>Thus the three stars! Because I can't enjoy a story where the final lines go something like this, "And so I learned that my husband was right all along..."<br><br>Seriously, people? I'm married. My husband hasn't been right since he signed those papers! It's a fact of life.<br><br>Married men are never right.<br><br>The end.<br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="7043106697872262337" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer198859183" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4115160807681036303"><b>5...HUGE...GIGANTIC...IMMENSE...<br/>STARS!<br/><br/>WOW! WOW! WOW!</b> I honestly don't know what to say about this book that hasn't already been said numerous times other than it's easily become my <b>FAVORITE</b> paranormal romance thus far. <b>There wasn't a single thing about this story that I didn't absolutely and completely love</b>. <br/><br/>I won't go into detail about the plot, the characters, or the writing; there are <b>plenty</b> of fantastic reviews already written that fully express my feelings, thoughts, and sentiments about th</span>
  <span id="freeText4115160807681036303" style="display:none"><b>5...HUGE...GIGANTIC...IMMENSE...<br />STARS!<br /><br />WOW! WOW! WOW!</b> I honestly don't know what to say about this book that hasn't already been said numerous times other than it's easily become my <b>FAVORITE</b> paranormal romance thus far. <b>There wasn't a single thing about this story that I didn't absolutely and completely love</b>. <br /><br />I won't go into detail about the plot, the characters, or the writing; there are <b>plenty</b> of fantastic reviews already written that fully express my feelings, thoughts, and sentiments about this fantastic book (series). <b>I will say, though, that <i>Slave to Sensation</i> had the perfect mixture of world building, character development, story depth, intrigue, action, eroticism, and romance.</b> Not once did I become frustrate or annoyed with the plot or the characters. Nope! I spent the whole book captivated, fascinated, and enthralled. I was unable to put it down. In fact, much to my family's dismay, I was so absorbed in the story that I read it in one sitting. <br /><br />I'm not sure why I waited so long to start this series because I knew it would be right up my alley. Now I understand why so many of my friends consider the Psy-Changeling series one of their favorite paranormal reads. If the rest of the books are anything like this one, there's no doubt this series will become my favorite in the paranormal genre. </span>
  <a data-text-id="4115160807681036303" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28967089-jessica-s-totally-over-the-top-book-obsession?shelf=dont-judge-a-book-by-its-ugly-cover">dont-judge-a-book-by-its-ugly-cover</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28967089-jessica-s-totally-over-the-top-book-obsession?shelf=listened-to-on-audio">listened-to-on-audio</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer908172436" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13213703825159264873"><b>4 Feels for the first time stars</b><br/><br/><a href='https://imgur.com/TEsYy8Z' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1509953996ra/24373075.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Slave to Sensation is my first book by Nalini Singh and I really enjoyed it. I know I have had this baby on my kindle for a few years now and I sit here and wonder why I waited so long to start this series. I loved the whole world set up. The Psy being all mind with great psychic powers, and no feelings , the Changelings being shifters that feel greatly, and of course the boring humans. I do wish there would have been a bit more paranormal world development as</span>
  <span id="freeText13213703825159264873" style="display:none"><b>4 Feels for the first time stars</b><br><br><a href="https://imgur.com/TEsYy8Z" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1509953996ra/24373075.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Slave to Sensation is my first book by Nalini Singh and I really enjoyed it. I know I have had this baby on my kindle for a few years now and I sit here and wonder why I waited so long to start this series. I loved the whole world set up. The Psy being all mind with great psychic powers, and no feelings , the Changelings being shifters that feel greatly, and of course the boring humans. I do wish there would have been a bit more paranormal world development as I would have liked to known things like..... how long do the para live, how do they know when they found their mates? How do go about mating? All these things were touched on in a glossed over kind of way. <br><br><a href="https://imgur.com/8ZZrL04" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1509953996ra/24373076.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Lucas was sexy as hell and full of life and passion, which made Sascha seem like a lump by comparison. I did end up warming up to Sascha as the book went on but at first she was so flat it was hard to connect to her. I loved Lucas and Sascha together. Although I did wish Lucas would have figured out she was his mate a little bit sooner. I also really liked the others in Lucas' pack and I liked Hawke and I really hope he gets a book. I sure he will since this series is so long. Slave to Sensation was a great start to the series. It got me hooked on the world and the secondary characters. I can't wait to start book two!</span>
  <a data-text-id="13213703825159264873" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText17679371102220824034" style="display:none"><b>tragically, this is gonna be a dnf for me</b><br /><br />i really wanted to like this because i really like nalini's writing and while the guild hunters series is not my favorite i figured maybe psy-changeling might be a game changer. and this is a first book in a series so i don't want to judge too harshly... but i don't think this is going to work for me. it's almost the antithesis to everything that paranormal is in my eyes: passionate, fated mates etc. with psy characters... they're emotionless or at least are supposed to be.<br /><br />and i guess you could argue that could make for some good tension but it just fell flat for me. i didn't like the heroine and the hero was very... basic alpha type. idk. maybe i'll try again with this series someday but i can't be bothered at the moment.</span>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/390501414?book_show_action=true">Aug 13, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Blacky *Romance Addict*" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Blacky *Romance Addict*" href="/user/show/8310179-blacky-romance-addict">Blacky *Romance Addict*</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer390501414" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14475406498247276198"><b>This book goes to one of the best pnr's I've ever read. The writing is phenomenal, so great that I knew just with the first book that I'll be reading all the others :)</b><br/><br/><br/>I first heard of this series a few months ago, and my reaction was like this: O.o Psychic people devoid of emotions and shape-shifters as couples <a href='http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&current=25918.gif' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/350916.gif' alt='Photobucket' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a> . I decided I definitely wasn't going to read something like that.<br/>I was VERY, very, very, very stupid. <a href='http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&current=280532.gif' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380387456ra/747474.gif' alt='Photobucket' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a> <a href='http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&current=280532.gif' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380387456ra/747474.gif' alt='Photobucket' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/><b>The story</b> very much remindes me of the movie "Equilibrium", in which t</span>
  <span id="freeText14475406498247276198" style="display:none"><b>This book goes to one of the best pnr's I've ever read. The writing is phenomenal, so great that I knew just with the first book that I'll be reading all the others :)</b><br><br><br>I first heard of this series a few months ago, and my reaction was like this: O.o Psychic people devoid of emotions and shape-shifters as couples <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=25918.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/350916.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> . I decided I definitely wasn't going to read something like that.<br>I was VERY, very, very, very stupid. <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=280532.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380387456ra/747474.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=280532.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380387456ra/747474.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><b>The story</b> very much remindes me of the movie "Equilibrium", in which the hero lives in a society where all humans are without emotions, he is a member of the highest authority, and he deals with extinguishing everything that might trigger an emotional response (great movie btw, one of my favorites, Christian Bale is awsome <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=836920.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/356484.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> )<br>Here the heroine is part of the Psy society, they are genetically modified humans with some amazing psychic abilities, but no notion of emotion. She was born different, and forced to hide her nature from everyone. Lucas is a changeling, a species of shifters, able to turn into animals at will. He is wild by nature and ruled by emotion, and he finds her irresistible. Being able to sense she's not the usuall Psy, he sets on seducing her for information <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=419790.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380385935i/745079.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><b>Their chemistry was off the fu*king charts!</b> I mean, wow! Sascha was constantly trying to keep her facade of calm and emotionless, and Lucas was constantly trying to break it. The touching, caressing, the dreams <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=72866.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/362766.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> simply HOT. I wanted to pet him myself <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=54273.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/352106.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> the fact that he's a shifter - didn't really bother me, in some books that part has an icky feel to it, but here it was perfectly ok :)<br><br>And so I have to say, this book is a beginning of an obsession, I can already tell <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=3402580550.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/362254.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> I love the style of writing, the world the author created has me in it's grip and I don't think it will let go untill I reach the final book.<br><br>BTW, Hawk was in this one, the alpha of the wolf pack, I sooo want to read him <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=bliss.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/357951.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=bliss.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/357951.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=bliss.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/357951.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

<div id="review_2410538346" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2410538346" />
    <a title="Sophia Triad" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/44642860-sophia-triad"><img alt="Sophia Triad" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1591419108p2/44642860.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2410538346?book_show_action=true">Jun 01, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sophia Triad" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sophia Triad" href="/user/show/44642860-sophia-triad">Sophia Triad</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=shifters">shifters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=1paranormal-lovestories">1paranormal-lovestories</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=leopards">leopards</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2410538346" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5536927812852415098"><b>Sascha Duncan (Psy) and Lucas Hunter (Changeling)</b><br/><br/><i>
  <b>This was about murder… and the greatest lie that had ever been perpetuated by a race upon its own kind.</b>
</i><br/><br/>This book is an impressive start to a series that I have a feeling that it will become one of my favourite PNR series.<br/><br/>Psy-world is an interesting different new world. I haven't read anything similar before to be honest. The Psy have great psychic powers, but not feelings or desires.<br/>They basically live in two worlds: <br/>1.	The real world which al</span>
  <span id="freeText5536927812852415098" style="display:none"><b>Sascha Duncan (Psy) and Lucas Hunter (Changeling)</b><br /><br /><i>
  <b>This was about murder… and the greatest lie that had ever been perpetuated by a race upon its own kind.</b>
</i><br /><br />This book is an impressive start to a series that I have a feeling that it will become one of my favourite PNR series.<br /><br />Psy-world is an interesting different new world. I haven't read anything similar before to be honest. The Psy have great psychic powers, but not feelings or desires.<br />They basically live in two worlds: <br />1.	The real world which also includes Changelings (shifters) and humans.<br />2.	The PsyNet which is like Internet, except it’s made up of minds, not computers. I would also compare it with the movie Matrix. It is actually a place where Psy “meet” and “socialize”.<br /><br />Shifters are the normal shifters that we meet in most PNR books. They can transform into animals and they live in packs. We learn about two packs:<br />1.	The DarkRiver leopard pack<br />2.	The SnowDancers wolf pack<br />These two packs coexist in neighbourhood grounds.<br /><br />In terms of mating, there can be only one lifemate for each Changeling.<br /><br />Lucas Hunter is the Alpha of DarkRiver pack and he is a black panther. He will meet Psy Sascha Duncan , while he tries to find the Psy killer who keeps butchering Changeling females. When another girl is taken, Lucas runs out of time.<br /><br />Sascha lately is not well. She is scared to death and she tries to hide it before she is locked away in a “rehabilitation facility”. Her main problem is that she has started having feelings, emotions, physical reactions in these emotions. This is not normal for a Psy. She is defective. The fact that she needs to work so closely to Changelings that they are overflowed with feelings and they are so close to their animal side, does not help.<br /><br />Gradually we will learn that Psy have secrets. Their own lack of emotions is a deception imposed to them in order to make them less dangerous.<br /><br />I enjoyed the writing style and the way the story and the world building is exploited. The mystery with the serial killer has a obvious solution, but I really did not mind this. I wad satisfied with everything else.<br /><br /><br />------------------------------------------<br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[2010: I think I will start this series. I heard it is good.<br />2012: Maybe this year, I will start it. It has shifters!<br />2013: Damn. I think I will try it next year. I have already started two new series.<br />2016: This is the year I will start this series. This January. After I finish this trilogy. And the new Black Dagger Legacy book. And maybe a couple of books I started last December.<br />2017: Why haven't I started this series yet? Why? Why? Why?<br />2018, January: I am definitely starting this series next month. Oh, look new books by Larissa Ione! Oh God!<br /><br />2018, June: I am officially declaring Psy-Changeling series my challenge for this summer!!! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></span>
  <a data-text-id="5536927812852415098" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <div class="elementListBrownSeparator"></div>



  <div class="friendReviews elementListBrown" >
    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_153746024" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/153746024" />
    <a title="Emily May" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4622890-emily-may"><img alt="Emily May" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1528390751p2/4622890.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/153746024?book_show_action=true">Mar 11, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Emily May" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Emily May" href="/user/show/4622890-emily-may">Emily May</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780575095663" href="/book/show/7179268-slave-to-sensation">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4622890-emily-may?shelf=pnr">pnr</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4622890-emily-may?shelf=2011">2011</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer153746024" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11122063330612807621">This book receives so many rave reviews that I guess I was just expecting a bit of something more. In fact, I was fully convinced before I started that I would probably give this book a 4 star rating, it just shows that I should stop making predictions - I'm usually wrong. I will say that I liked it enough to take a curious look into the rest of the series, it's not as if they're particularly difficult to read so I don't mind as much suffering through them. <br/><br/>The thing about this novel was that I </span>
  <span id="freeText11122063330612807621" style="display:none">This book receives so many rave reviews that I guess I was just expecting a bit of something more. In fact, I was fully convinced before I started that I would probably give this book a 4 star rating, it just shows that I should stop making predictions - I'm usually wrong. I will say that I liked it enough to take a curious look into the rest of the series, it's not as if they're particularly difficult to read so I don't mind as much suffering through them. <br /><br />The thing about this novel was that I found the first half to be at complete odds with the second half. I thought the story focus shifted, the strong heroine became weak and whiny, and the male love interest who I had previously thought was sexy to death became a misogynistic control freak. Yeah, he did somewhat recover what I'd liked about him towards the end... but I felt that he could never be the character I originally thought he was after he pushed Sascha (the aforementioned heroine) around for trying to decide something for herself. What is with romance novels today? Particularly paranormal romance novels, it seems as if they all contain a relationship where the man completely controls the woman and her lifestyle. Please say it's not just me who thinks these kind of relationships are stomach-turning?<br /><br />I get the alpha-male attraction. I get the bad boy attraction. But that's all a sex issue... a guy playing mr dominant in the bedroom is one thing, but it's something else entirely when he thinks he can say who the woman is allowed to speak to, where she goes, what she wears. It makes me cringe. The point is that Lucas (mr hero guy) started off as sexy-in-a-suit, he identified Sascha as a powerful woman from a powerful and dangerous race that should not be taken lightly. They start off as equals and their flirtations and attraction to each other is hot to the point where I was on edge all the time and wondering where we would go next. But...<br /><br />The exact minute that Lucas discovers that the attraction is mutual, he has sex with her and, from then on, attempts to completely take over her life. That's what I hated. They went to bed together (admittedly - very hot!) and the next morning he woke up an entirely different character. And not only him, but her too. She is from the Psy, a race of creatures that are just as powerful, if not more so, than the Changelings but as soon as he takes her virginity she turns into a dithering mass of patheticness. Aside from being annoying, it also didn't flow or make any sense at all.<br /><br />The story that formed the bigger picture was fairly good. You can sort of imagine a future where a superior race has been developed, each member completely immune to the ultimate weakness: emotion. They are programmed to be this way and let only facts and logic rule their minds... then, of course, amongst the ranks of this new race is one with the unforgivable defect - Sascha, who is starting to feel. This is a good idea and I was loving it until everything turned upside down halfway through. It's bad enough to be let down by any book that you were expecting to be good, but it's even worse to be let down in the middle of said book when the first half had been so promising. Ah well, I'll still see what the other books in this series bring and I hope they don't all fall into the same pattern.</span>
  <a data-text-id="11122063330612807621" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1103307665" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1103307665" />
    <a title="✘✘ Sarah ✘✘ (former Nefarious Breeder of Murderous Crustaceans)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7298986-sarah-former-nefarious-breeder-of-murderous-crustaceans"><img alt="✘✘ Sarah ✘✘ (former Nefarious Breeder of Murderous Crustaceans)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1587115780p2/7298986.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1103307665?book_show_action=true">Nov 11, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="✘✘ Sarah ✘✘ (former Nefarious Breeder of Murderous Crustaceans)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="✘✘ Sarah ✘✘ (former Nefarious Breeder of Murderous Crustaceans)" href="/user/show/7298986-sarah-former-nefarious-breeder-of-murderous-crustaceans">✘✘ Sarah ✘✘ (former Nefarious Breeder of Murderous Crustaceans)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/6479112-slave-to-sensation">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7298986-sarah-former-nefarious-breeder-of-murderous-crustaceans?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7298986-sarah-former-nefarious-breeder-of-murderous-crustaceans?shelf=2014">2014</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7298986-sarah-former-nefarious-breeder-of-murderous-crustaceans?shelf=don-t-kill-it-with-fire-pnr">don-t-kill-it-with-fire-pnr</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1103307665" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer882798714032417761"><b>I'm not usually a fan of romance and I'm pretty new to PNR</b> so I didn't really know what to expect from this book. I've had the whole series on my Kindle for some time but wasn't planning on reading it until <b><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/3344685-sarah' rel='nofollow noopener'>Sarah</a> and <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/4255477-angela' rel='nofollow noopener'>Angela</a> ganged up on me.</b> Ah, good old peer pressure never fails! So I decided to give the series a try <b>despite the cheesy titles and ridiculous book covers</b>. Well, I have to say, thank you so much ladies because <b>this was fun!</b><br/><br/><b>I expected silly romance but what did I get?</b> Complex, well t</span>
  <span id="freeText882798714032417761" style="display:none"><b>I'm not usually a fan of romance and I'm pretty new to PNR</b> so I didn't really know what to expect from this book. I've had the whole series on my Kindle for some time but wasn't planning on reading it until <b><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/3344685-sarah" rel="nofollow noopener">Sarah</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/4255477-angela" rel="nofollow noopener">Angela</a> ganged up on me.</b> Ah, good old peer pressure never fails! So I decided to give the series a try <b>despite the cheesy titles and ridiculous book covers</b>. Well, I have to say, thank you so much ladies because <b>this was fun!</b><br /><br /><b>I expected silly romance but what did I get?</b> Complex, well thought-out, <b>refreshingly original world building.</b> I've always been a shifter fan (what can I say? I can't resist domineering/possessive Alphas who need taming^^) and the idea of <b>mixing them up with the Psy</b> (a race with psychic abilities) was just pure brilliance. Cold, analytical Psy vs emotional, tactile, unpredictable Changelings? <b>This is one world with huge potential</b>. I can't wait to see what Singh comes up with in the next instalments. There are so many possibilities here that I can't see how this series could ever get boring <b>*crosses fingers*</b> If I wasn't feeling so lazy I'd give more details about the world but I am so if you want to know more about just go read the book:p Trust me when I say that this is good. <b>Really good.</b><br /><br /><b>I think the main weakness of the book is the plot.</b> Hold on, no that's not right. It's not the plot, it's the resolution. No, that's not right either. The plot is fast-paced and pretty good but its resolution is disappointing because of the <b>culprit's identity.</b> I guessed who it was very early on. I kept hoping there would be a twist and it would turn out to be someone else but it didn't happen. This is part of the reason I didn't give this book a 4. <b>It was still a very entertaining story though.</b> Singh's writing flows effortlessly despite the changes in POV. They can ruin a book when badly handled but here they only <b>add to the story dynamics.</b><br /><br /><b>The characters?</b> <b>Sascha is great.</b> I just love how complex her character is, the way she constantly fights with herself and <b>struggles with her arising emotions.</b> She's very straightforward, strong-willed and isn't easily pushed around. That's my kind of girl! <b>Lucas is the designated possessive/stubborn/sexy Alpha.</b> I have to admit that he's a bit on the light side as Alphas go and not as aggravating or overbearing as I expected. It doesn't mean I didn't like him though and <b>I wouldn't mind having this particular cat to tame;o) </b><br /><br /><b>As I said before I'm not very big on romance</b> but I have to say this one was handled fairly well by Singh as it wasn't too overwhelming. <b>It's more insta-lust than insta-love</b> which fits the story perfectly. The relationship between Sascha &amp; Lucas slowly evolves throughout the book and although you know from the start where it's heading Singh manages to keep things interesting until the end. <b>Okay, so it takes a while to get to the steamy sex scenes</b> but the dream trick adds just enough lust and sexual tension to make it worth the wait. <b>And yes, the sex scenes are pretty hot^^</b><br /><br /><b>Now the ending of the book is a bit too HEA for my taste</b> but I guess it's pretty much a requirement in this genre so I'll try to get over it.<br /><br /><b>A surprisingly good read which leaves me wanting more. Next please!</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="882798714032417761" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1025192879" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1025192879" />
    <a title="Choko" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/27962805-choko"><img alt="Choko" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1475642755p2/27962805.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1025192879?book_show_action=true">Aug 12, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Choko" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Choko" href="/user/show/27962805-choko">Choko</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27962805-choko?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1025192879" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14101505138371986527"><b>*** 3.66 ***<br/><br/>A buddy read with the Paranormal Romance friends at BB&B! </b><br/><br/>The world is divided. It is populated by Psy and Changelings, and human races, all different in their ways of life, mores and codes, things they hold dear. We learn nothing about the humans here, unfortunately. The Psy have been bread out of emotions, which are considered as weaknesses and flaws, a hurdle keeping them away from perfection. The Psy hold power by "linking" into a network of all Psy individual minds, feeding thei</span>
  <span id="freeText14101505138371986527" style="display:none"><b>*** 3.66 ***<br /><br />A buddy read with the Paranormal Romance friends at BB&amp;B! </b><br /><br />The world is divided. It is populated by Psy and Changelings, and human races, all different in their ways of life, mores and codes, things they hold dear. We learn nothing about the humans here, unfortunately. The Psy have been bread out of emotions, which are considered as weaknesses and flaws, a hurdle keeping them away from perfection. The Psy hold power by "linking" into a network of all Psy individual minds, feeding their mental state and supporting as well as spying on all of them. If a Psy is detected to "feel", they are either "rehabilitated" for life, or killed... The Changelings on the other hand, OWN their emotions, experience all the levels of closeness to each-other, and live to what they see as the fullest. With the severe differences between them, it is easy to see how hostile the two can be to each-other. It gets even worse when women from the packs of Changelings began being found dead, obviously killed by Psy, but a murderous Psy should not exist... What has happen??? This is what the Alpha of the Panther pack Lucas has determined to find out and avenge! <br /><br />Sasha thinks she is dying... She is a Psy, a daughter of one of the high Counsel, but she is broken... Something is very, very wrong with her - she FEEL!!! (the horror!!!) She has been trying to hide it for a while, trying to belong, but lately it has been getting harder and harder... She has a chance to prove herself to her mother by working on a business deal with the Changelings on a building project with DarkRiver. This is when she met Lucas and her life changed for ever more... <br /><br />This is a love story. A Changeling (shifter) and a Psy find out about each-other and their different worlds. But even more than a love story, this is about the human attributes we put value to and what devoting to one extreme or another can do to our way of life. It is the constant battle we live between the thinking of our minds and the urges of our hearts... It is about the conflict of being who and what we are... <br /><br />I enjoyed this book more than I thought I would. Yes, it is a typical Paranormal Romance, and yes, it has many of the tropes this genre relies on, but after all, isn't that why we come back for more??? Why fix it when it works, right?:):):) I am planning on finishing this series, so this is the best recommendation I can give:) <br /><br />I wish you all happy reading and many, many good books to come!!! </span>
  <a data-text-id="14101505138371986527" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer13300291145605689127">The cover of this book? The name of this book? I was like no-way-Jose. But, then Jose said to me, "jilly, stop being a snob. Your friends all loved this book for a reason. Now, go read it." That Jose is so freaking smart.<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1443241546i/16338808.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><i>and a cheerful mofo too!</i><br/><br/>Anyhoo, the world-building in this book is fun.   <span id="freeText13300291145605689127" style="display:none">The cover of this book? The name of this book? I was like no-way-Jose. But, then Jose said to me, "jilly, stop being a snob. Your friends all loved this book for a reason. Now, go read it." That Jose is so freaking smart.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1443241546i/16338808.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>and a cheerful mofo too!</i><br><br>Anyhoo, the world-building in this book is fun. We have humans (boooring), Changelings (shapeshifters), and people called "Psy's" who are psychically gifted and connected to each other through a network in their brains. The Psy race undergoes a treatment from youth to erase all emotions from them. They are supposed to be walking computers, basically.<br><br>This story is about a Psy with all the feels. And, that's just wrong! She needs to keep her feels to herself or the other Psy's will kill her. No broken Psy's allowed.<br><br>But, our broken Psy girl meets a Changeling guy and all the feels break loose. They have to work together AND solve a murder-mystery before the next girl is killed. Duh! Obviously there is a murderer loose that only our broken Psy girl can find.<br><br>Oh yeah, and this is all set in the future, so hovercars!! Yeah baby! Finally! I've been waiting my whole life for a freaking hovercar. They'll probably come out the year after I'm dead, so I'm all about the hovercars in books. I guess you could call me a hoverhead.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1443241546ra/16338809.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i> if they do come out in my lifetime, this is what I'll be able to afford!</i><br><br>I think this is the start of something good.</span>

<div id="review_1581216328" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1581216328" />
    <a title="Kate" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13603287-kate"><img alt="Kate" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1531664914p2/13603287.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1581216328?book_show_action=true">Mar 16, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kate" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kate" href="/user/show/13603287-kate">Kate</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/11325410-slave-to-sensation">review of another edition</a>


          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Kate by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/14430576-love2read-heas-anne">☆.。.:*・°☆Love2Read♡HEAs☆.。.:*・°☆ {Anne}</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13603287-kate?shelf=5-stars">5-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13603287-kate?shelf=ebooks">ebooks</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13603287-kate?shelf=2020-read">2020-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13603287-kate?shelf=guys-be-a-steaming">guys-be-a-steaming</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13603287-kate?shelf=broody-alphas">broody-alphas</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13603287-kate?shelf=dystopian-and-post-apoclayptic">dystopian-and-post-apoclayptic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13603287-kate?shelf=bliming-hilarious">bliming-hilarious</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13603287-kate?shelf=pnr-uf-fantasy-steampunk">pnr-uf-fantasy-steampunk</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13603287-kate?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13603287-kate?shelf=bad-boys">bad-boys</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1581216328" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3747572015784538577"><b>1st read - 27th March 2016, 2nd read - 29th May 2017, 3rd read - 3rd May 2020<br/><br/>One of the best series in PNR out there. <br/><br/>5 Unfortunately I can’t give it more as Goodreads won’t let me Stars.<br/><br/>When you read a lot of pnr/uf you need something that stands out of the mass otherwise you think that you are reading the same things. Finding something as exceptional, unique and remarkable as what I read with a Slave to Sensation is rare. <br/><br/>I worship the ground that Ms. Singh has walked on since the Guild Hunter</b></span>
  <span id="freeText3747572015784538577" style="display:none"><b>1st read - 27th March 2016, 2nd read - 29th May 2017, 3rd read - 3rd May 2020<br /><br />One of the best series in PNR out there. <br /><br />5 Unfortunately I can’t give it more as Goodreads won’t let me Stars.<br /><br />When you read a lot of pnr/uf you need something that stands out of the mass otherwise you think that you are reading the same things. Finding something as exceptional, unique and remarkable as what I read with a Slave to Sensation is rare. <br /><br />I worship the ground that Ms. Singh has walked on since the Guild Hunter series. Admittedly I read both a sample of Angel Blood &amp; Slave to Sensation a couple of years ago and I wasn’t impressed but now I am and I freely admit when I am wrong. <br /><br />With a first introduction to a new world it is hard to not overwhelm the reader with too much information. But then there is also a lacking in the world that you want the reader to picture in their imagination. Ms. Singh feeds enough to keep us sated but keeps us curious about the world that we have entered and that we want to continue reading without food, drink and going for a pee. <br />Imagine a world with no emotion, no rage, no jealousy, no envy, no happiness and certainly no love at all. <br /><br />Sascha Duncan a Psy cardinal is different to the other Psy. For years she has been protecting her shields not to expose her flaws to her mother, the council and all other Psy beings. She is beginning to fail. Sascha is a fantastic main character, she is strong, sassy but still has a certain vulnerability about her that you just can’t help but not like. <br /><br />Lucas Hunter a changeling and an alpha to the DarkRiver pack, he is the youngest alpha, strong possessive and I loved all of his character. He is interesting, we see what he sees and what he feels. <br /><br />The Psy and the Changeling are entering a business deal and Sascha is going to be Lucas associate. Lucas as well as his animal are fascinated with Sascha as she acts like a Psy but there are signs that not all is what it seems. Sascha feels even more then she should when she is around Lucas. Fear, Amusement, Hunger, Lust, Desire, Need. <br /><br />Changeling women are being kidnapped and murdered and that other a certain period of time. One of his pack died and they want to find the killer. Sascha &amp; Lucas start to trust one another and Sasha has such a strong character development. <br /><br />They are great together, Sascha &amp; Lucas have something special. Their sexual encounters occur in dreams to begin with but they have such a strong connection in such a short time span and it didn’t feel forced. On top of that there was attraction but never instalove. <br /><br />They complement each other. They have sparks, fireworks the whole shebang. <br /><br />“We’re way beyond skin privileges, darling”<br /><br />But there were also times where there seemed to be the possibility that it wouldn’t work between them. <br /><br />“I wish I’d been born in another time, another place. Then maybe I could’ve escaped fate… maybe I could’ve been your darling.”<br /><br />There are funny moments in the book as well. <br /><br />Her eyes narrowed. “We’re going to have to talk about this dominant streak of yours.” “It’s not a dominant streak. It’s all me.”<br /><br />Sascha goes against the system and is willing to pay the consequences for her desires. What makes Sascha special will most likely get her killed. <br /><br />There were twists and turns to the book and my main concern was how it was going to be pulled off with the Psynet etc. Colour me surprised I loved that frigging ending. <br /><br />I see so many possibilities for this world and one I can’t wait for is Hawke from the SnowDancers.</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="3747572015784538577" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer175596255" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4075861901301881975"><br/><b>5 Stars!!! Fantastic! What took me so long to read this?!?! </b><br/><br/>Out of all the paranormal creatures, shifters are my favorite, and <i>Slave to Sensation</i>, captured the true nature of these sexy human/beasts!!! <b>RAWRRRRR!!</b> The merging of the unfeeling, emotionless citizens of the Psy community, and the touchy feely, possessive Changeling pack members, made for a very sensual, fascinating, and extremely gratifying read. Amazing world building, memorable characters...that got under my skin, terrific dialogu</span>
  <span id="freeText4075861901301881975" style="display:none"><br /><b>5 Stars!!! Fantastic! What took me so long to read this?!?! </b><br /><br />Out of all the paranormal creatures, shifters are my favorite, and <i>Slave to Sensation</i>, captured the true nature of these sexy human/beasts!!! <b>RAWRRRRR!!</b> The merging of the unfeeling, emotionless citizens of the Psy community, and the touchy feely, possessive Changeling pack members, made for a very sensual, fascinating, and extremely gratifying read. Amazing world building, memorable characters...that got under my skin, terrific dialogue, and a detailed, yet interesting storyline, make this book a stand-out! I did a combination of reading and listened on audio, doesn’t matter the format you choose, it’s well worth your time. <br /><br />Thank you to Jayne, Kris, and Autumn! They pointed me in the direction of this series, and have been encouraging me to read it! I took the plunge girls…I’m totally immersed in the Psy-Changeling world! I can’t wait to get my hands on the next book! <br /></span>
