Except for Sascha and a few others! <br/><br/>Anyway, Psy's are made to feel no emotion, void, nothing, zip, zilch. But . . . Sascha has feelings and if they find out she is "broken" they will rehabilitate her or kill her. REALLY? <br/><br/><b>Because I'm broken. And the Psy don't allow borken creatures to live.</b><br/><br/>The Changelings are the shifters and they are cool and then there are humans but they don't take on a big role in the book. <br/><br/>Sascha is sent by her mom who is on the Psy Council </span>
  <span id="freeText1864153411178327589" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1471484064i/20060333._SY540_.jpg" alt=" : " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Well I think the Psy's are jerks. Except for Sascha and a few others! <br><br>Anyway, Psy's are made to feel no emotion, void, nothing, zip, zilch. But . . . Sascha has feelings and if they find out she is "broken" they will rehabilitate her or kill her. REALLY? <br><br><b>Because I'm broken. And the Psy don't allow borken creatures to live.</b><br><br>The Changelings are the shifters and they are cool and then there are humans but they don't take on a big role in the book. <br><br>Sascha is sent by her mom who is on the Psy Council to oversee some business dealings they are doing with the Changelings. Sascha is going to be spending a lot of time with the alpha of the DarkRiver leopard pack, Lucas and he's yummy. =) And they are also working with the SnowDancers pack which is the wolf changelings. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1471484064i/20060334._SX540_.jpg" alt=" : " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And Lucas has some kind of feelings for Sascha that he doesn't understand because they all hate the Psy. As I have said, Sascha isn't like the others, she's "broken" and I hate they think of themselves that way when they are actually normal. But I digress! Lucas and his panther self start having feelings for Sascha, he wants her as his and Sascha has feelings for Lucas. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1471484064ra/20060335.gif" alt=" " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I felt really sorry for Sascha because she was having so much fun being away from the Psy. She didn't know what it was like to touch someone. She didn't know what CHOCOLATE tasted like because they have not need for that, only balanced meals. It would suck to be a Psy and have actual feeling like Sascha and be scared to death at all times that they will find out and kill you! <br><br>But for now she is having a wonderful time with the changelings. Then she finds out about this serial killer that has been taking changeling women for quite some time and they are Psy. She refuses to believe this at first because it never showed up in any of the networks. The changelings finally convince her that is is a Psy because they could smell them around the mutilated bodies. Sascha decides to help find out who the killer is and she does and I knew who it was :-D <br><br>And all the while Sascha and Lucas fall in love with each other and have some passionate moments if you know what I mean. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1471484064i/20060336._SX540_.jpg" alt=" : " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The ending was good, the book was good and I look forward to more of the series. <br><br>MY BLOG: <a href="http://melissa413readsalot.blogspot.com/2016/08/slave-to-sensation-by-nalini-singh.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Melissa Martin's Reading List</a></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/40406887?book_show_action=true">Dec 18, 2008</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Shawna" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Shawna" href="/user/show/1802746-shawna">Shawna</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

           <span class="uitext reviewText">PNR fans</span></div>

    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Shawna by: </span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1802746-shawna?shelf=2009-reads">2009-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1802746-shawna?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1802746-shawna?shelf=hero-i-wanna-marry">hero-i-wanna-marry</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1802746-shawna?shelf=hero-alpha%E2%80%8E">hero-alpha‎</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1802746-shawna?shelf=hero-abused-scarred-tortured-angst">hero-abused-scarred-tortured-angst</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1802746-shawna?shelf=i-read-own-faves-keepers">i-read-own-faves-keepers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1802746-shawna?shelf=hero-besotted-so-smitten-its-sexy">hero-besotted-so-smitten-its-sexy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1802746-shawna?shelf=favorite-romance-series">favorite-romance-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1802746-shawna?shelf=scifi-futuristic-fantasy-misc-pnr">scifi-futuristic-fantasy-misc-pnr</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer40406887" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer167862365694189259">4 ½-5 stars – Paranormal Romance<br/><br/>Since I’m a little late jumping on the <i>Psy-Changeling</i> series fan bandwagon, there probably isn’t much to add that hasn’t already been said about this fantastic series. <b>Slave to Sensation</b> is a fabulous debut that sets the foundation for the war between the emotionless, cold, psychically powerful Psy race and the Changelings in the year 2079.<br/><br/>In a world where the Psy have enforced a mandatory code of Silence that denies and prohibits all emotion, Psy member Sascha Du</span>
  <span id="freeText167862365694189259" style="display:none">4 ½-5 stars – Paranormal Romance<br /><br />Since I’m a little late jumping on the <i>Psy-Changeling</i> series fan bandwagon, there probably isn’t much to add that hasn’t already been said about this fantastic series. <b>Slave to Sensation</b> is a fabulous debut that sets the foundation for the war between the emotionless, cold, psychically powerful Psy race and the Changelings in the year 2079.<br /><br />In a world where the Psy have enforced a mandatory code of Silence that denies and prohibits all emotion, Psy member Sascha Duncan has had to conceal her “flawed” makeup out of fear of discovery and forced ‘rehabilitation’. When she works alongside Lucas Hunter, the alpha leader of the Changeling (shifters that are both human and animal) DarkRiver leopard pack, to find the Psy killer responsible for brutally butchering several Changeling women, including his packmate, it becomes impossible to resist her long denied emotions and feelings. Sascha calls to the panther in Lucas, and he brings out her pent up passion. The two engage in a dangerous, consuming affair that could forever alter the precarious co-existence between Psy-Changelings. <br /> <br />Lucas and Sascha’s relationship is sexy, emotionally stimulating, loving, and scorching hot. Singh’s writing is top-notch, and she does a great job balancing the world building and romance. It’s a great first book in a unique, erotic paranormal series about the cold Psy race ruled by the gifts of the mind and the Changeling race whose strength comes from the heart. 4 ½ stars...almost 5 stars!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="167862365694189259" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4019749635947871579">(Edited to add further thoughts.)<br/><br/><b>5 Stars</b> - <i>Also reviewed at: <a href='http://ladyjaynesreadingden.blogspot.com/2011/08/review-slace-to-sensation-1-psy.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>Lady Jayne's Reading Den</a><br/></i><blockquote>
<b>*~*Slave to Sensation *~*</b><br/><br/>Touching fingertips,<br/>To ice-cold lips,<br/>The skimming touch,<br/>Sensations, too much;<br/>The brushing thigh,<br/>Escaping sigh,<br/>The softest whispers,<br/>Sends primal shivers;<br/>Barely leashed control,<br/>Of a fractured soul,<br/>The heat of skin,<br/>Burst flames within;<br/>Instinctive artistry,<br/>Reactive chemistry,<br/>The ragged breath,<br/>Cerebral death;<br/>Who thought such bliss,<br/>In just one kiss?<br/>Now, his changeling touch, she craves,<br/>Has sh</blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText4019749635947871579" style="display:none">(Edited to add further thoughts.)<br><br><b>5 Stars</b> - <i>Also reviewed at: <a href="http://ladyjaynesreadingden.blogspot.com/2011/08/review-slace-to-sensation-1-psy.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Lady Jayne's Reading Den</a><br></i><blockquote>
<b>*~*Slave to Sensation *~*</b><br><br>Touching fingertips,<br>To ice-cold lips,<br>The skimming touch,<br>Sensations, too much;<br>The brushing thigh,<br>Escaping sigh,<br>The softest whispers,<br>Sends primal shivers;<br>Barely leashed control,<br>Of a fractured soul,<br>The heat of skin,<br>Burst flames within;<br>Instinctive artistry,<br>Reactive chemistry,<br>The ragged breath,<br>Cerebral death;<br>Who thought such bliss,<br>In just one kiss?<br>Now, his changeling touch, she craves,<br>Has she become sensation’s slave?<br><br>(by J.M.A. a.k.a. Lady Jayne, 12th August 2011)<br><br>~*~*~*~*~*~</blockquote> Nooo… <b>
  <i>Slave to Sensation</i>
</b> isn’t a book of poetry. I had drafted a review for this, but unfortunately, it was on my laptop, which was among the items stolen in a recent break-in. And somehow, when I sat down to re-write this “review”, this poem came out. Sorry. If you are one of the few people (like me) who has not read this series yet, <i>PLEASE</i> do not judge it based on my humble “ode” to it! LOL<br><br><i>Slave to Sensation</i> is the first book in the stimulating Paranormal Romance (PNR) Psy/Changeling series by Fijian-New Zealander author, Nalini Singh. I kept seeing this series being hailed as a favourite PNR amongst my Goodreads friends. I must say, now I know the appeal! What a deliciously enjoyable first book in a series! This book was published in 2006, so yes, I've been slow to jump on this bandwagon...but that's okay, that just means I have a lot of Psy/Changeling books to enjoy! *grins*<br><br>While Nalini Singh seduced me, with this first taste, to crave more of the books in this series, this poem was my attempt to capture how the sexy, tactile and sensually primal Changeling, Lucas Hunter, a panther who is the Alpha of the DarkRiver leopard pack, managed to overwhelm Sascha Duncan, of the cold Psy race, with sensation – something “unnatural” to the Psy, who do not touch. <i>Slave to Sensation</i> is indeed an apt title.<br><br>I’ve always had a fascination for stories with characters who have psychic abilities, and have developed, in the last few years, a love of the sexy animalism of shape-shifters. And this book combines both loves! I loved this remarkably interesting, detailed and imaginative world that Nalini Singh created - Bravo, Ms. Singh! The writing and the story were thought-provoking and evocative.<br><br>This story is set in 2079 in San Francisco and its surrounds, where co-exist, though not without its tensions, three main groups of people: The Psy - a psychically advanced and logical race who conditioned emotions out of their society through a program called “Silence”, which was instigated in 1969, in an effort to reduce the high incidence of insanity and violence in the Psy population, and who consider themselves the “superior” race; the Changelings - the instinctual, emotional, territorial and sensual shape-shifters, made up of various animal packs, who are cunning and underestimated by the Psy; and the humans - there is only mention of them in this book, though I am told that there will be human characters in later books. <br><br>I loved that there was suspense and mystery in this story – of a serial killer targeting Changeling women. Lucas and Sascha meet as part of a Psy-Changeling business venture and end up working together to solve the mystery.<br><br>I loved, and connected with, the character of Sascha, who is terrified about being found out as a “flawed” Psy and as a matter of survival struggles to hold on to her fragile mask of a calm, cool, and collected Psy. Sascha is no “typical” Psy and the ability she possesses is one that I wish I had. <br><br>And Lucas? Mmm, mmm, mmmm… He was dangerously sexy <i>hawt</i>, with a tortured past, determined to claim Sascha as his mate, and he was just so <i>there</i> for Sascha. Purrrrs….<br><br>The only <i>wee</i> issue I had with the book…which is my problem, really… was with the concept of the “PsyNet”, which, while incredibly fascinating, was a little confusing, especially with the projection of a “shield” within a “shield” within a “shield” and the computronics imagery – I’m not tech or computer savvy - which reminded me of <i>Matrix</i> meets <i>Tron</i> meets <i>Inception</i>. Brain buzzingly cool.<br><br>I loved the cast of characters of the Changelings and the two packs introduced in this book – the DarkRiver pack (leopards) and the SnowDancers (wolves). I had recently seen the prevalent love for Hawke, the Alpha of the wolf pack, and from his introduction in this book, I could already understand the fascination with him and am excited to get to his book….which unfortunately isn’t until Book 10! I was also fascinated with Vaughn, from the leopard pack, who wears his beast closer to the surface than others in his pack, and just <i>had</i> to read his book, which was next in the series, <b>
  <i>Visions of Heat</i>
</b>, straight away!<br><br><b>If you are one of the few people who haven’t read this series yet, make sure you pick up <i>Slave to Sensation</i> ASAP!!!</b> <blockquote>
  <i>"He tasted better than her dreams, as rich and delectable as the most exquisite chocolate, as exotic as the panther he was.”</i>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380339948i/696531.jpg" width="280" height="370" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Lucas Hunter - Lusciously dangerous to the senses <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380339948i/696532.jpg" width="280" height="370" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>A panther and Alpha of the DarkRiver Leopards<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380339948i/696533._SY540_.jpg" width="260" height="360" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Sascha Duncan - An unraveling cardinal Psy, <br>with night-sky eyes	 <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380339948i/696534.jpg" width="350" height="250" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Sascha's animal instincts are awakened by Lucas<br><br>~*~*~*~*~*~<br><br><b>Edited to add - Thoughts on "A Society Without Emotion?":</b> <br><br>I mentioned in this review that this book (well, the series) is “thought-provoking” and just wanted to share some of the thoughts it “provoked”. <br><br>I’ve been thinking about how interesting it is that the Psy race has so many people of interracial genetic background, as a majority of them are “test tube babies”. For example, Sascha is of mixed Asiatic (Japanese) and Anglo-Indian descent. It seems that the prejudices for the Psy people, however, run not in the colour of one’s skin, but rather in the fact that one has less cerebral development/ lack of psychic ability / is an emotional being. The Psy consider themselves “superior” to the Changelings, who they consider only a step above animals and humans.<br><br>Then I thought about the kind of extreme society the Psy have created by eliminating emotion. It seems, though, that the Psy Council, the ruling body of the Psy, can be ruthless. Is ruthlessness a result of the absence of emotion? “Ruthless” is defined in the dictionary as “having no compassion or pity”. The Psy, having conditioned emotions out of their race through the “Silence Protocol”, have no compassion or pity.<br><br>But… the Changelings, who are emotional beings, are also capable of being ruthless. This is mostly evident in their ruthlessness in vengeance. In this sense, it is the presence of the emotion of rage and drive for revenge, which may cause them to be “ruthless” – it is their overwhelming emotion which may render them unable to feel compassion or pity... or maybe it is just a choice not to. <br><br>One of the questions posed by this book is: Has the Psy decision, based on logical reasoning, to eliminate emotion in order to eradicate violence and mental illness, instead created the very monsters the Psy sought to control? So, to feel or not to feel? Crimes of passion versus the cold killings of sociopaths?<br><br>Also, what about the Psy’s “indifference” as opposed to “ruthlessness” – will apathy be the downfall of the Psy?<br><br>I just know that I wouldn’t want to live in a world without emotion. But I would like to live in a world without violence. With or without emotion, is violence an inevitable part of the human condition?<br><br>These are just some of the thoughts I had - mostly just rhetorical questions! LOL<br><br>~*~*~*~*~*~<br><br><b>Psy/Changeling Series Reading Order:</b><br><br>1. Slave to Sensation<br>1.5 "The Cannibal Princess" - Free short story:<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.nalinisingh.com/freebies.php#princess">http://www.nalinisingh.com/freebies.p...</a> - (<a>Review here</a>)<br>2. Visions of Heat - (<a>Review here</a>)<br>3. Caressed By Ice - To be reviewed. <br>4. Mine to Possess (<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/124090396" rel="nofollow noopener">Review here</a>) <br>5. Hostage to Pleasure - To be reviewed.<br>5.5 "A Gift for Kit" - Free short story: <br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.nalinisingh.com/freebies.php#gift">http://www.nalinisingh.com/freebies.p...</a><br>6. Branded By Fire<br>7. Blaze of Memory<br>8. Bonds of Justice <br>9. Play of Passion<br>10. Kiss of Snow<br><br>And there are also stand-alone novellas:<br>1. "Beat of Temptation" in An Enchanted Season<br>2. "Stroke of Enticement" in The Magical Christmas Cat<br>3. "Whisper of Sin" in Burning Up<br><br>But if you wish to read in strict chronological order, see Nalini Singh's website (link to the page here): <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.nalinisingh.com/psybehind.php">http://www.nalinisingh.com/psybehind.php</a><br><br><br><i>COPYRIGHT DISCLAIMER: I do not hold the copyright to any of the images used in this review. They are posted to add visuals to the review and for fun. If any of these images are yours and you would like me to remove them, please let me know, and I will do so as soon as possible. If I can identify the copyright, I will do so.</i></span>

<div id="review_36760033" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/36760033" />
    <a title=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books"><img alt=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1403239075p2/1570669.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/36760033?book_show_action=true">Nov 02, 2008</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" class="user" itemprop="url" name=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" href="/user/show/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books"> Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">fans of paranormal romance, fans of shapeshifter paranormal romance</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=aar-top-100-romance">aar-top-100-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=alpha-hero">alpha-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=enemies-to-lovers">enemies-to-lovers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=fated-to-be-mated">fated-to-be-mated</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=part-of-a-series">part-of-a-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=futuristic">futuristic</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=hero-to-die-for">hero-to-die-for</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer36760033" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3474754913966372728">Boy, I am so glad that I had read one of Nalini Singh's Silhouette Desire novels, and was searching for some more paranormal romances to read and finally picked this one up by her. I kicked myself for having waited so long. I loved this book. Lucas is to die for. He's totally yum. I loved the combination of paranormal with science fiction. I typically find science fiction a little bit dry at times, since I am more of a fantasy person. But there is a perfect mix of science fiction and paranormal </span>
  <span id="freeText3474754913966372728" style="display:none">Boy, I am so glad that I had read one of Nalini Singh's Silhouette Desire novels, and was searching for some more paranormal romances to read and finally picked this one up by her. I kicked myself for having waited so long. I loved this book. Lucas is to die for. He's totally yum. I loved the combination of paranormal with science fiction. I typically find science fiction a little bit dry at times, since I am more of a fantasy person. But there is a perfect mix of science fiction and paranormal fantasy in this book. I love how Singh created this future world where there are three types of people: Psy (completely cerebral with enhanced psychic abilities, reject emotions), Changeling (part human/part animal, embrace emotion), and Humans. This story focuses mainly on the Psy and Changeling dynamic. In Singh's Psy/Changeling world, race is not an issue. Most of the characters are of various ethnic backgrounds and interracial relationships have no stigma. I found this very refreshing. Singh's worldbuilding is so plausible that you don't doubt that in the future humans can reject emotions and build their psychic abilities to the penultimate. It takes a leap of faith to believe in changelings (shapeshifters), but if you don't have that, then you shouldn't be reading this book. If you do, then hang on. <br /><br />Lucas doesn't care for the Psy. To him, they are soul-less, conscienceless beings. But for the sake of business, he deals with the Psy. When he meets Sasha, he is drawn to her. She doesn't have the stink of Psy (they have a cold, deadly metallic smell to the Changeling breed). The Psy are hated because they have ruthlessly gained control of society and are not above killing those who stand in their way. So at first, Lucas is off-put by his attraction to Sasha. Not for long though. It doesn't take this very confident cat to recognizes she is his mate, and he doesn't wait much longer to claim her as his. Their relationship was blistering hot. I was fanning myself during the love scenes. Sasha has had issues with her powers, having blackouts and feeling scary losses of control of her emotions that she has been hiding from her parental units, because Psy who lose control and break Silence (the lack of emotion) are sent for rehabilitation, eventually becoming mindless vegetables. Lucas inspires violent passion in her which is unheard of in a Psy. She has no idea how to deal with this, yet she is required to work with him. Lucas seems to enjoy teasing her and inspiring sensual feelings in her. I loved their interactions. <br /><br /> I am a big fan of shapeshifter stories, and I loved the descriptions of the pack of big cats of which Lucas is the alpha. I also enjoyed reading about their new allies, the pack of wolf shapeshifters, who is alphaed by the enigmatic Hawke (can't wait for his story). Really, I cannot recommend this series enough. If you are like me and typically get a little bored with hard science fiction, but want to expand your horizons, I would suggest this book and the Psy/Changeling series. The romance is the focus, and the science fiction elements teamed with paranormal is like marshmallow sauce on chocolate, just the right touch. Singh is a gifted author who has won my devotion as a fan.</span>
  <a data-text-id="3474754913966372728" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_779210606" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/779210606" />
    <a title="Jessica ❁ ➳ Silverbow ➳ ❁ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10336538-jessica-silverbow"><img alt="Jessica ❁ ➳ Silverbow ➳ ❁ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1393785730p2/10336538.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/779210606?book_show_action=true">Dec 02, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jessica ❁ ➳ Silverbow ➳ ❁ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jessica ❁ ➳ Silverbow ➳ ❁ " href="/user/show/10336538-jessica-silverbow">Jessica ❁ ➳ Silverbow ➳ ❁ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=weres-shapeshifters">weres-shapeshifters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=science-fiction">science-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=esp">esp</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer779210606" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2241594046807629194">It's been a little over a year since I read this the first time. I wasn't really impressed, but I just finished the Guild Hunter series (LOVED it), so I decided to give Singh's other series another shot.<br/><br/>I'm glad I did.<br/><br/>I might have been in a reading slump the last time I read <i>Slave to Sensation</i>, or maybe I just couldn't get past the cheesy (and let's be real--it <i>is</i> cheesy) title and book cover. Whatever it was, second time was the (a?) charm. <br/><br/>Sascha is a Psy. That means she's been trained to be a</span>
  <span id="freeText2241594046807629194" style="display:none">It's been a little over a year since I read this the first time. I wasn't really impressed, but I just finished the Guild Hunter series (LOVED it), so I decided to give Singh's other series another shot.<br /><br />I'm glad I did.<br /><br />I might have been in a reading slump the last time I read <i>Slave to Sensation</i>, or maybe I just couldn't get past the cheesy (and let's be real--it <i>is</i> cheesy) title and book cover. Whatever it was, second time was the (a?) charm. <br /><br />Sascha is a Psy. That means she's been trained to be a Vulcan. But Psys, unlike Vulcans who as a race eventually "evolved" past emotional reactions, are born <i>with</i> emotions and are brainwashed out of feeling them. Or at least they're supposed to be. If a Psy is resistant to the brainwashing, they are rehabilitated. And by "rehabilitated" I mean lobotomized. <br /><br />Lucas is a Hunter and the Alpha of the leopard pack in California. He is Changling. Changlings and Psys do <i>not</i> play well together. They have nothing in common. Psys are cold, emotionless robots while Changlings are vibrant and passionate and <i>alive</i>. Even the smell of a Psy stinks to a Changling nose.<br /><br />Until Lucas meets Sascha. He immediately senses she is more than the average Psy.<br /><br />But he can't think about that too much b/c he's using their business arrangement to gather information about the Psy race in order to catch a Psy serial killer.<br /><br />Romance and havoc ensue before the token para-romance happy ending. <br /><br />That's what I love about para-romance. No delayed gratification. A happy ending is coming and soon.</span>
  <a data-text-id="2241594046807629194" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1738482154" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer3331340635059618596"><blockquote>
  <b>⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱*Still liked it*⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱</b>
</blockquote><br/><b>
  <u>Re-read: 29.10.2018</u>
</b><br/>I got curious as to why I had liked this book the first time reading as I couldn't remember a thing about it or why I stopped. The book center around ‘flawed’ Psy <b>Sascha Duncan</b> (26) and alpha changeling; a black panther (or a leopard?), <b>Lucas Hunter</b> (33). Lucas is hunting a Psy killer, and he plans to use Sascha do get an 'in', however, Sascha is not what it seems. Sascha is broken, her mind-shields are crumbling and she has little time left</span>
  <span id="freeText3331340635059618596" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱*Still liked it*⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱</b>
</blockquote><br><b>
  <u>Re-read: 29.10.2018</u>
</b><br>I got curious as to why I had liked this book the first time reading as I couldn't remember a thing about it or why I stopped. The book center around ‘flawed’ Psy <b>Sascha Duncan</b> (26) and alpha changeling; a black panther (or a leopard?), <b>Lucas Hunter</b> (33). Lucas is hunting a Psy killer, and he plans to use Sascha do get an 'in', however, Sascha is not what it seems. Sascha is broken, her mind-shields are crumbling and she has little time left, however, Lucas makes her want more. <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Scooting forward on little baby paws, one of the cubs licked the tip of her nose in a quick movement. She was so startled that she blurted out, “What does that mean?”<br>“It means he likes you.” Lucas tugged at her plait. “But that doesn’t matter to you, does it?”<br>“No.” She wished he’d stop touching her. Not because she didn’t like it but because she liked it far too much. It made her hunger for things that could never be hers. And if someone went hungry for too long, they started to starve. Started to hurt.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1540796296i/26514882.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>Overall, I refused to stop reading until I was done</b>. It's seven in the morning and I'm super tired, and here I am writing a review that probably doesn't make sense. The book was long, filled with a whole lot information but I still liked it. Now I can see why I liked it the first time. Sascha is such a likable character and Lucas is sorta perfect: commanding, powerful, dominant, possessive and overprotective. All things I love. I do believe that the reason I didn't continue the series was simply because I hate - or used to - getting a new couple each book. It's so stressful. Anyways, I'm gonna try reading book two.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>She was his and he was hers. They had under-the-skin privileges.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><b><u>Other characters</u>:</b><br>↦ <b>Nikita Duncan</b>, Sascha's mother and a member of the Psy Council. She became a Councilor at forty.<br>↦ <b>Dorian</b>, a latent leopard. Something had gone wrong in the womb and he’d been born changeling in all ways except one-he lacked the ability to shift forms. His sister, Kylie, was the one who was killed and butchered six months ago and Lucas is on the hunt for her murderer.<br>↦ <b>Tamsyn ‘Tammy’</b>, a packmate of Lucas and a healer. Nate, her mate? Her kids, <b>Roman</b> and <b>Julian</b>, leopard cubs<br>↦ <b>Kit Monaghan</b>, packmate of Lucas. He had the scent of a future alpha. Kit works part-time as a general assistant. <b>Rina</b> (21), his older sister, a curvaceous, sensual female with the rank of soldier.<br>↦ <b>Zara</b> is the designer, a distant cousin-wildcat who works in a leopard business (Lucas's) because she's the best. She was marked by the scent of Lucas and his sentinels so that enemies and friends alike knew who she belonged to.<br>↦ Psy Councilor <b>Santano Enrique</b> (60), an academic. He was an off-the-scale Tk-Psy with so much telekinetic power that he could crush Sascha without blinking. There were 7 councilors; <b>Marshall Hyde</b>, <b>Tatiana Rika-Smythe</b>, <b>Ming LeBon</b>, <b>Shoshanna Scott</b> and <b>Henry Scott</b> and Sascha's mother.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“As for what Hunters do, we hunt down rogues.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>↦ <b>Nate</b>, <b>Vaughn</b> (30), a jaguar, <b>Clay</b> (34), <b>Mercy</b> (28), and <b>Dorian</b>, a latent leopard (?), Lucas' sentinels. They were the toughest members of the pack. In a one-on-one fight, every one of them would lose to Lucas. But together they were formidable. As Lucas had told Sascha, if he broke vital Pack laws they’d take him down. Until then, they were his absolutely. Vaughn was Lucas’s closest friend and quite possibly the only male capable of holding the pack together if Lucas were killed, in spite of the fact that, to the leopards, he didn’t have the scent of an alpha. Nate was already on the lookout for his replacement. Upon retirement as a sentinel, he would become one of Lucas’s advisors, his rank undiminished.<br>↦ <b>Clay Bennett</b>, Lucas' construction supervisor.<br>↦ <b>Tatiana Rika-Smythe</b> (35), her and the Rika-Smythes are Sascha's family primary business rivals.<br>↦ <b>Ria</b>, Lucas' administrative assistant and human; mated to a DarkRiver leopard for the past seven years.<br>↦ <b>Hawke</b>, the ruthless alpha of the SnowDancers (wolves). His lieutenants, <b>Indigo</b> and <b>Riley</b>.<br>↦ <b>Sienna Lauren</b>, her brother, <b>Toby</b>.<br>↦ <b>Walker Lauren</b>, Sienna and Toby are the children of his deceased sister. His daughter, <b>Marlee</b>. <b>Judd Lauren</b>, Walker’s brother.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>According to her information, Hunter had become the only ruling alpha in the DarkRiver leopard pack at twenty-three years of age. In the ten years since, DarkRiver had consolidated its hold over San Francisco and surrounding regions to the extent that they were now the dominant predators in the area. Outside changelings who wanted to work, live, or play in DarkRiver territory had to receive their permission. If they didn’t, changeling territorial law went into force and the outcome was savage.<br>What had made Sascha’s eyes open wide in her first reading of this material was that DarkRiver had negotiated a mutual nonaggression pact with the SnowDancers, the wolf pack that controlled the rest of California. Since the SnowDancers were known to be vicious and unforgiving to anyone who dared rise to power in their territory, it made her wonder at DarkRiver’s civilized image. No one survived the wolves by playing nice.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445268775i/16623124.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b><u>First read review</u>:</b><br><b><u>Simply put</u>:</b> I adored <b>Sascha Duncan</b> and I kinda loved <b>Lucas Hunter</b>, and together they were awesome. I actually liked the story, though the book was a bit too long. <i>Nalini Singh</i> is a brilliant writer, still her <i>Guild Hunter</i> series is still my favorite (at least Raphael &amp; Elena's books). I am not sure if I'll continue the series since I think there's new couple for each book (?), but who knows? The side characters were interesting... <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I wish I’d been born in another time, another place. Then maybe I could’ve escaped fate… maybe I could’ve been your darling.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><b><u>Quick basic facts</u>:</b><br><b>Genre</b>: - (Adult) Paranormal Romance<br><b>Series</b>: - Series, Book One <br><b>Love triangle?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Cheating?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>HEA?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Yes. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Favorite character?</b> - Lucas Hunter.<br><b>Would I read more by this author/or of series?</b> - Yes.<br><b>Would I recommend this book/series?</b> - Yes.<br><b>Will I read this again in the future?</b> - Who knows?<br><b>Rating</b> - 3.5 stars.</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/75717037" />
    <a title="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish"><img alt="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1398981306p2/1113032.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/75717037?book_show_action=true">Oct 25, 2009</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" class="user" itemprop="url" name="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" href="/user/show/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish">UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audible Audio " href="/book/show/13418976-slave-to-sensation">review of another edition</a>


          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/5477946-kristen">Kristen</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=author-nalini-singh">author-nalini-singh</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=format-audio-via-audible">format-audio-via-audible</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=5-stars">5-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=kidnapped-hostage">kidnapped-hostage</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=first-in-series-trilogy-duet">first-in-series-trilogy-duet</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=own-have-read">own-have-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=format-paperback">format-paperback</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=2014-reads">2014-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=emotionally-scarred">emotionally-scarred</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer75717037" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18374343921876209970"><br/><b>4.5 Holy Hot Shifters stars!</b><br/><br/><i>Slave to Sensation</i> is the first book in Nalini Singh’s wildly popular <i>Psy-Changling</i> series. This world she’s created is exciting, passionate, poignant… it’s like none I’ve ever read before.<br/><br/><b>Description…</b><blockquote>Dive into a world torn apart by a powerful race with phenomenal powers of the mind—and none of the heart…<br/><br/>In a world that denies emotions, where the ruling Psy punish any sign of desire, Sascha Duncan must conceal the feelings that brand her as flawed. To reveal them woul</blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText18374343921876209970" style="display:none"><br /><b>4.5 Holy Hot Shifters stars!</b><br /><br /><i>Slave to Sensation</i> is the first book in Nalini Singh’s wildly popular <i>Psy-Changling</i> series. This world she’s created is exciting, passionate, poignant… it’s like none I’ve ever read before.<br /><br /><b>Description…</b><blockquote>Dive into a world torn apart by a powerful race with phenomenal powers of the mind—and none of the heart…<br /><br />In a world that denies emotions, where the ruling Psy punish any sign of desire, Sascha Duncan must conceal the feelings that brand her as flawed. To reveal them would be to sentence herself to the horror of “rehabilitation”— the complete psychic erasure of everything she ever was….<br /><br />Both human and animal, Lucas Hunter is a Changeling hungry for the very sensations the Psy disdain. After centuries of uneasy co-existence, these two races are now on the verge of war over the brutal murders of several Changeling women. Lucas is determined to find the Psy killer who butchered his packmate, and Sascha is his ticket into their closely guarded society. But he soon discovers that this ice-cold Psy is very capable of passion—and that the animal in him is fascinated by her. Caught between their conflicting worlds, Lucas and Sascha must remain bound to their identities—or sacrifice everything for a taste of darkest temptation…</blockquote><b>My review…</b><br /><br />I’ll start by saying that I’ve had this book sitting on my shelf for years, but never felt the pull to read it. My awesome Goodreads friend, Kristen, and I were chatting on the phone and she started raving about the audio version so, me being a recent convert to audio books, decided to give it a listen.<br /><br />Sweet Mary! Am I ever glad I did!!<br /><br />There are so many awesome reviews already written, but even though everything that <i>needs</i> to be said has <i>already </i>been said, I want to share my thoughts, too. Like I mentioned above; it’s an exciting, passionate, poignant world, and it’s so unique that if you asked me to compare it to some other series, or another author’s writing, I wouldn’t be able to do it. PNR and Fantasy are what lay the foundation for this world, and even though I am not a fan of the Fantasy genre, this worked for me, no doubt about it. A big part of why it worked is that the characters are people whose lives make this a very emotionally charged, poignant read, and those characters are people whose stories demand to be told.<br /><br />Angela Dawe is the narrator and she did a fantastic job of showing the emotions these people feel; frustration, helplessness, pain… and yet hope, strength and joy. <br /><br />I hear these stories just get better and better and I can<i>not </i>wait to find out for myself!<br /><br />Thanks for the not so gentle nudge to listen, Kristen! YOU ROCK!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="18374343921876209970" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1705045148" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1705045148" />
    <a title="Elizabeth Hunter" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5645632-elizabeth-hunter"><img alt="Elizabeth Hunter" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1510179280p2/5645632.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1705045148?book_show_action=true">Jul 21, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Elizabeth Hunter" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Elizabeth Hunter" href="/user/show/5645632-elizabeth-hunter">Elizabeth Hunter</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5645632-elizabeth-hunter?shelf=will-re-read">will-re-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5645632-elizabeth-hunter?shelf=incredible-worldbuilding">incredible-worldbuilding</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5645632-elizabeth-hunter?shelf=crying-because-i-didn-t-write-it">crying-because-i-didn-t-write-it</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1705045148" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3890145165338768563">It's somewhat mind-boggling to me that I have not reviewed this series here because this is one of my all time favorites. So this review is WAY overdue. I'll review this book and then give you a brief overview of my view on the series, which is something like fourteen books now and I'm still not bored.<br/><br/><b>Fourteen books. Still not bored. Yes, you read that correctly.</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1469126472ra/19783985.gif' width='300' height='150' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>First off, like other reviewers have said, ignore the cheesy US cover. It makes this book look like a typical paranormal romance (not </span>
  <span id="freeText3890145165338768563" style="display:none">It's somewhat mind-boggling to me that I have not reviewed this series here because this is one of my all time favorites. So this review is WAY overdue. I'll review this book and then give you a brief overview of my view on the series, which is something like fourteen books now and I'm still not bored.<br><br><b>Fourteen books. Still not bored. Yes, you read that correctly.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1469126472ra/19783985.gif" width="300" height="150" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>First off, like other reviewers have said, ignore the cheesy US cover. It makes this book look like a typical paranormal romance (not that I don't love those) but this book is so far from typical. Singh has created a world in the Psy-Changling series that defies categories. <b>It's paranormal. It's SciFi. It's alternate history. And it's totally believable. The world-building is stellar and the romances are unique and character-driven. No cookie-cutter plots here.</b><br><br>Imagine a world—our world—split into three subspecies of humans. Regular old folks like you and me, Psy humans who have supernatural mental abilities like telepathy and teleportation, and Changelings who shapeshift. Imagine these three groups have existed for most of history and interacted, all adding depth and their unique talents to the world. Interested yet?<br><br>Now imagine one of those groups, the Psy, cut themselves off from the others because of fear of their own abilities, madness, and violence. Cut themselves off and cut all emotion out of their lives and the lives of their children, instituting a program called Silence. The Psy join or they die. They cannot exist without the others of their race, and they do not believe their race will survive if they allow emotion to exist. This happens to this world seventy years or so before the start of <i>Slave to Sensation</i> and some of the prologues that Singh writes throughout the series describing the process and progression of Silence are some of the most chilling scenes and scenarios that I have read.<br><br>The heroine of <i>Slave to Sensation</i> is a powerful Psy named Sasha Duncan, but she is struggling at the start of the book. In fact, she's pretty sure she is going insane. Why? Because despite her years of intense conditioning under Silence, Sasha is starting to FEEL. And that, for the Psy, means mental (and possibly physical) death from a Council that controls their race with an iron hand. Sasha would know, because her own mother is part of that Council.<br><br>The hero of the book is Lucas Hunter, the alpha of a leopard Changeling pack near San Francisco. He's ambitious, smart, and ruthlessly protective. When he meets Sasha, something about her rubs him the wrong way... aaaaand the right way! IfyouknowwhatImean. AndIthinkyoudo.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1469126472ra/19783986.gif" width="300" height="150" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>But Psy don't feel. They're basically human robots. Right? RIGHT?<br><br>(Of course they're not robots, and this series has enough steam to power a decent sized generator. In fact, the eventual Psy heroes have all been favorites. JUDD. VASIK. OMG KALEB I CAN'T EVEN.)<br><br>So Sasha is in trouble! But she's no helpless heroine. Lucas wants Sasha big time. He's a total alpha-type hero, but he's also a sneaky, sneaky cat. This couple, and this book, defy the expectations we've come to have about paranormal romance. Their relationship LITERALLY CHANGES THE WORLD. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1469125938ra/19783934.gif" width="300" height="150" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>(But, you know, in a good way.)<br><br>And the series doesn't stop. This is probably my favorite paranormal romance series for several reasons. The world never stands still. It only grows in depth and complexity. This is political, smart, action-packed, deep ROMANCE. The relationships are never easy, and they're never the same. Each couple stands out in a different way, making this one series I've re-read multiple times and will continue to re-read. <br><br>It's also a really diverse world, which I appreciate, and the settings hop all over the globe, though a lot of the action is centered in Northern California.<br><br><b>To sum up: read this book, read this series. I love it, and I think my readers (especially those who like the Elemental series) will really enjoy Nalini Singh's work.</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="3890145165338768563" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/381896281?book_show_action=true">Aug 01, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Dija" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Dija" href="/user/show/2857113-dija">Dija</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer381896281" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16130847495111369458"><i>*Buddy read with Sarah. You can read her review <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/135237176' rel='nofollow noopener'>here</a>.*</i><br/><br/><b>What I expected: </b><br/><b>1.</b> Lust at first sight leading to lots of sexy times that magically develop into love overnight.<br/><b>2.</b> A boring plot. <br/><b>3.</b> A <s>lickable</s> likable yet cliched hero.<br/><b>4.</b> A nice but entirely forgettable heroine.<br/><b>5.</b> A hundred eyeroll-worthy and puke-inducing moments.<br/><br/><b>What I got: </b><br/><b>1.</b> A beautiful romance that slowly develops (emphasis on slowly) into true love on the basis of friendship, understanding, communication, respect, and a healthy dose o</span>
  <span id="freeText16130847495111369458" style="display:none"><i>*Buddy read with Sarah. You can read her review <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/135237176" rel="nofollow noopener">here</a>.*</i><br /><br /><b>What I expected: </b><br /><b>1.</b> Lust at first sight leading to lots of sexy times that magically develop into love overnight.<br /><b>2.</b> A boring plot. <br /><b>3.</b> A <s>lickable</s> likable yet cliched hero.<br /><b>4.</b> A nice but entirely forgettable heroine.<br /><b>5.</b> A hundred eyeroll-worthy and puke-inducing moments.<br /><br /><b>What I got: </b><br /><b>1.</b> A beautiful romance that slowly develops (emphasis on slowly) into true love on the basis of friendship, understanding, communication, respect, and a healthy dose of chemistry. <br /><b>2.</b> An extremely interesting plot with some of the greatest world-building I've ever come across in PNR.<br /><b>3.</b> A delicious hero I adored. <br /><b>4.</b> A lonely and heartbroken heroine I really liked. <br /><b>5.</b> Witty banter and thoroughly engaging dialogue...for the first half. The second part did have those above-mentioned moments, but they were only about two dozen in number. Yippee.<br /><br />To sum it up, I loved the beginning of the story and it only got better and better. Up until the middle, when Sascha and Lucas get together for real. It simply went downhill from there and everything was surrounded by So. Much. Drama! What completely killed the 4-stars I was leaning towards was Sascha's self-sacrificing act towards the end. I can't stand those, and hers was one of the most melodramatic of the lot. <br /><br />That aside, I love nearly all of the supporting members of the cast. Right now, I'm most intrigued by Hawke and Brenna. I have around ten more books to go before getting to know Hawke properly, but Brenna's story isn't too far off and I can't wait to read it. But before that, I plan on reading Tammy and Nate's novella, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/188275.An_Enchanted_Season__Includes_Psy_Changeling___0_5__Murphy_Sisters___1_" title="An Enchanted Season (Includes Psy-Changeling, #0.5; Murphy Sisters, #1) by Maggie Shayne" rel="nofollow noopener">An Enchanted Season</a>, because I loved these two much more than Lucas and Sascha. <br /><br /><b>For more reviews, visit my <a href="http://zombiehazard.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">blog</a>. </b></span>
  <a data-text-id="16130847495111369458" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_62249743" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/62249743" />
    <a title="valee" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2320890-valee"><img alt="valee" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1443365004p2/2320890.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/62249743?book_show_action=true">Jul 05, 2009</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="valee" class="user" itemprop="url" name="valee" href="/user/show/2320890-valee">valee</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780575095663" href="/book/show/7179268-slave-to-sensation">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2320890-valee?shelf=amazing-pnr-romance">amazing-pnr-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2320890-valee?shelf=fav-series-and-reads">fav-series-and-reads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer62249743" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9197180118222398435"><b>There's just not any other book more worth of a re-read than this one!</b> I'm not kidding. OMG, I mean, I had loved it the first time I read it but nothing close as the way I felt about it this second time. I had completely forgot what it was to be so lost in a book that you didn't notice at all the pass of time. I just couldn't put it down, and every time I checked my clock I was so sure only an hour had passed but so much more had... *blushing, seriously, I completely lost track of time. But what</span>
  <span id="freeText9197180118222398435" style="display:none"><b>There's just not any other book more worth of a re-read than this one!</b> I'm not kidding. OMG, I mean, I had loved it the first time I read it but nothing close as the way I felt about it this second time. I had completely forgot what it was to be so lost in a book that you didn't notice at all the pass of time. I just couldn't put it down, and every time I checked my clock I was so sure only an hour had passed but so much more had... *blushing, seriously, I completely lost track of time. But what I'm trying to tell you all is that this is a book that <b>NEEDS</b> to be read at least 2 times. The first time I read it I really couldn't enjoyed it as much as this because I was trying too hard to understand all the plot and world building. This is a very complex series with too much new information to us and it takes a lot to completely understand it all. For me, it was a lot to take in the first time I read it so I couldn't' appreciate Lucas and Sascha's relationship as I did this time.<br /><br />What a complex book, I just didn't remember so many things happen in it. There's just so much to take in. First we have an introduction to a whole new world with beings so unknown to us that it will take you some time only to grab the smallest of knowledge about them. I'm talking about <b>the PSY: </b>They are not really human, but they look like them. The difference is that they are introduced to the SILENT treatment since they are born. This means no feelings for them at all, no love, no hate, no selfishness, no caring, nothing at all. The reason for this was that if you don't feel you won't kill nor destruct, nor do any harm. The PSY species has their power in their minds, some are telekinetic, some can create mental viruses while others can kill others just with a thought. Such is their power that they have become the more powerful beings on Earth. But this is about to change as the PsyNet is getting fractured and many Psy are changing, becoming broken. The PSYs who rule this species, the Council, are suppose to fix every problem that appears. They are the most powerful PSYs and they have complete power to rule as they feel like doing, so what is it to stop them from doing the wrong thing? PSYs are suppose to do the logical thing, the right one, so nobody expects the Council to act wrongly because they shouldn't be able to do so, they are PSYs after all. But if some PSY are starting to break, how can you put all your trust and give free power to PSYs who are not being controlled by anybody else than themselves? <br /><br />As if getting to know this amazing and complex species wasn't enough, we get to read about<b> the CHANGELINGS</b>, beings who are not completely human but are half animal. Lucas is a changeling Alpha who would do anything to protect his people. While he is at the top of the command chain, there are others on his pack that could be able to take him down merging forces if he goes rouge; but they never would as they love their alpha and would do anything to protect him. He has won his place and has everyone's loyalty. Lucas get's introduce to Sascha after starting business negotiations with the PSYs. Both will get to know better and realize none was what they thought would really be. So many things happen, so many mysteries get resolve while others begin. Two races are now on the verge of war, things start to change, the Changeling wont allow so much power to the PSY.Where will Sascha stand? How can a PSY change if she isn't even suppose to feel anything at all? How will Lucas be able to make her understand?<br /><br />So many things happen in this series that it's not possible not to ADORE it. This is the series with the best plot, no doubts what so ever, you just can't help to get sucked into it. The need to understand and get to know more about everything is overwhelming. <b>I'm just happy I made this re-read because now I was finally able to understand everything and get to appreciate the book way more.</b> I really wanna recommend you guys a 2nd read, definitely the best course of action with this book.</span>
  <a data-text-id="9197180118222398435" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer209403958135073337"><b>5 ***AMAZING*** STARS!!!<br/><br/>Lucas Hunter is my new Book Boyfriend!!<br/><br/><i>“I’m possessive and I’m territorial. Since the dawn of Silence, emotions have b</b></span>
  <span id="freeText209403958135073337" style="display:none"><b>5 ***AMAZING*** STARS!!!<br><br>Lucas Hunter is my new Book Boyfriend!!<br><br><i>“I’m possessive and I’m territorial. Can you handle that?” </i><br><br>Lucas Hunter<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1551721151i/27152824._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="600" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I finally got my hands on book one of my favorite paranormal series and it was Awesome!!!<br><br>Lucas is the alpha of the leopard pack and I'm officially in love. He's dominant and affectionate and so damn sexy with all that yummy testosterone!! Oh and I'm a total sucker for a scarred hero!!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1551637792i/27148645._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Can I just say how much I loved Sasha. Since the dawn of Silence, emotions have been banned and the Psy are cold, sterile, and emotionless. Sasha is Psy and was raised to believe she's flawed. She believes her feelings are a weakness, not a strength. <br><br>Sasha Duncan<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1551720991i/27152818._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It takes a delicious alpha like Lucas to pull Sasha out of her shell. It was wonderful to see how it all started with Lucas, Hawke and the Psy. I love this series and reading book 1 makes me wanna re-read the entire series.</b></span>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/474654606?book_show_action=true">Dec 10, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jo ★The Book Sloth★" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jo ★The Book Sloth★" href="/user/show/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth">Jo ★The Book Sloth★</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

            Shelves:

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer474654606" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7530314301878397240"><b>5 Wild Stars</b><br/><br/>This is gonna be short because I have the whole series to re-read to get to the last one.<br/><br/><b>Why I love this book</b><br/><br/>1) <i>Lucas</i> is HOT! As an Alpha he is possessive, protective, domineering, caring. All that in just the right measure to be hot and not overbearing.<br/><br/>2) <i>Sascha</i> is so brave. I can't even imagine how hard it must be growing up with secrets that will get you killed when you know that your mind is intimatelly connected to those you're keeping your secrets from.<br/><br/>3) <i>The packs</i>. The packs a</span>
  <span id="freeText7530314301878397240" style="display:none"><b>5 Wild Stars</b><br /><br />This is gonna be short because I have the whole series to re-read to get to the last one.<br /><br /><b>Why I love this book</b><br /><br />1) <i>Lucas</i> is HOT! As an Alpha he is possessive, protective, domineering, caring. All that in just the right measure to be hot and not overbearing.<br /><br />2) <i>Sascha</i> is so brave. I can't even imagine how hard it must be growing up with secrets that will get you killed when you know that your mind is intimatelly connected to those you're keeping your secrets from.<br /><br />3) <i>The packs</i>. The packs are full of interesting people. I can't wait to re-read their books!!<br /><br />That's all for now. A nice love story, unique worldbuilding, shapeshifters and a psychotic serial killer. What's not to love?<br /><br /><b>31/08/2014 Re-read</b><br /><br />This scene is just so heartbreaking!<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“Sometimes I remember that I can't always protect those I love." Under his fingers, her hair was soft and silky.<br />She didn't try to tell him that he wasn't God, that he couldn't protect everyone. He knew that. <br />But knowing and believing were two different things. What she did say succeeded in stopping his heart. "I wish you'd love me."<br />"Why?"<br />"Because then maybe you could protect me, too" Haunting sorrow whispered through her tone.”</i>
</b></span>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('7pNNI3DKb4chLrLHzJUVXHcOioljkV+ocukh+9BY4bUdreq02P2GYXwmd0tjduGKPqO6/3RweaUOVq9PRy3FSA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('6yJvGeP4m3+1zAddOjMiSe2pkqIbAWArwL82WSFo18sYHMiOS89ymejEwtGV0NafpASi1AzgRia8ALjtth3zNg==')})
  }
//]]>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer13592023853085332864">I've been writing as long as I can remember and all of my stories always held a thread of romance (even when I was writing about a prince who could shoot lasers out of his eyes). I love creating unique characters, love giving them happy endings and I even love the voices in my head. There's no other job I would rather be doing. In September 2002, when I got the call that Silhouette Desire wanted t</span>
  <span id="freeText13592023853085332864" style="display:none">I've been writing as long as I can remember and all of my stories always held a thread of romance (even when I was writing about a prince who could shoot lasers out of his eyes). I love creating unique characters, love giving them happy endings and I even love the voices in my head. There's no other job I would rather be doing. In September 2002, when I got the call that Silhouette Desire wanted to buy my first book, Desert Warrior, it was a dream come true. I hope to continue living the dream until I keel over of old age on my keyboard.<br /><br /><br />I was born in Fiji and raised in New Zealand. I also spent three years living and working in Japan, during which time I took the chance to travel around Asia. I’m back in New Zealand now, but I’m always plotting new trips. If you’d like to see some of my travel snapshots, have a look at the Travel Diary page (updated every month).<br /><br />So far, I've worked as a lawyer, a librarian, a candy factory general hand, a bank temp and an English teacher and not necessarily in that order. Some might call that inconsistency but I call it grist for the writer's mill.<br /><br /></span>
